## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the rate of change of concentration (dA/dt) as a function of time and concentration in a chemical reaction. This is a classic chemical kinetics problem where the rate law describes how the reaction rate depends on the concentration of reactants, potentially with various orders and mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (rate proportional to concentration)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (rate proportional to square of concentration)
- nth-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate dependence)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (forward and reverse first-order reactions)
- Autocatalytic reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (product-catalyzed reaction)
- Second-order with equilibrium: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 + c1 * A + c2 (quadratic rate with equilibrium correction)
- Inhibition kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A / (1 + c1 * A) (substrate inhibition or saturation)
- Substrate inhibition: dA_dt = c0 * A / (1 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2) (non-monotonic rate with inhibition at high concentration)
- Time-dependent deactivation: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (catalyst deactivation over time)
- Consecutive reaction rate: dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) + c2 * exp(c3 * t) (intermediate species in consecutive reactions)
- Mixed-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (fractional order with constant offset)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (A**c1 + c2) (sigmoidal rate dependence on concentration)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative rate proportional to concentration power → nth-order irreversible decay: dA_dt = -c * A^n
- Rate that changes sign at a specific concentration → reversible reaction with equilibrium: includes both positive and negative linear/polynomial terms in A
- Rate with maximum at intermediate concentration → autocatalytic or substrate-inhibition mechanism: A*(c-A) or A/(1+cA^2)
- Rate independent of time but dependent on A → autonomous ODE, pure rate law without explicit time dependence
- Exponential time dependence in rate → catalyst deactivation, photodegradation, or time-varying external conditions
- Rational function of A → enzyme-like or surface-catalyzed mechanism with saturation
- Product of A with a polynomial in A → multi-step or complex reaction mechanism
- Rate approaching zero as A approaches zero → conservation-consistent kinetics without spontaneous generation

Matched candidates: ["A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)"]

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three terms:
1. A quadratic term: `-c₀*A²`
2. An exponential decay term: `-c₂*A*exp(-c₃*t)` (linear in A, exponential in t)
3. A cosine of log term: `c₄*cos(log(A + 1))`

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Key basis functions in GT:** `A²`, `A*exp(αt)`, `cos(log(A+1))`

I'll focus on candidates that could potentially match these three basis functions.

### Candidate 1: `A*c0 + A^c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6)`
- Has `A*exp(c3*t)` ✓ (if c1=1, but then A^c1*c2*exp = A*c2*exp, losing A²)
- If c1=2: `A²*c2*exp(c3*t)` - but GT has `A²` without exp(t)
- `sin(A*c5 + c6)` ≠ `cos(log(A+1))`
- Cannot match. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: `A⁵*c0*exp(c1*t) + A²*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5 + c6`
- Has `A²` ✓, `A*exp(c4*t)` ✓, but missing `cos(log(A+1))`. Has extra `A⁵*exp`, `A`, constant terms.
- Setting c0=0 eliminates A⁵ term. Left with `A²*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5 + c6`
- This is polynomial + exp, cannot produce `cos(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidates 3, 5, 21, 28, 29, 73, 79: Rational forms with `A` terms
These simplify to forms like `c/denominator + A*exp + A*c + ...` — polynomial/rational in A with exp(t). None can produce `cos(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]** for all.

### Candidate 4: `(A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*(c4*exp(c2*t)+1)*log(A*c5+1) + c6)/(c4*exp(c2*t)+1)`
Simplifies to: `A*c0/(c4*exp+1) + A*c1*exp/(c4*exp+1) + c3*log(A*c5+1) + c6/(c4*exp+1)`
= `A*(c0 + c1*exp)/(c4*exp+1) + c3*log(A*c5+1) + c6/(c4*exp+1)`
Has `log(A+c)` not `cos(log(A+c))`. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 6: Similar to 4 but with `log(A²*c5+1)`. Still log, not cos(log). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 7: `(c0 + (c1*exp(c2*t)+1)*(A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A^c5*c6))/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c1*exp+1) + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A^c5*c6`
With c0=0: `A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A^c5*c6`. Missing cos(log). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidates 8-14, 16-18, 23-36, 43, 45, 50, 54, 57, 62, 63, 70, 72: 
These contain combinations of polynomials, exp, log, sin(A*c), exp(A*c), but none have `cos(log(A+c))` or `sin(log(A+c))`. **[NO MATCH]** for all.

### Candidate 19: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7)`
- `A*exp(c1*t)` ✓ for the exp term
- `sin(c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7)` with c5=1, c7=π/2, c6=1: `cos(log(A+1))` ✓
- But needs `A²` term. Only has `A*c2`. Cannot produce A². **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 68: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8)`
- `sin(c6*log(A*c7+1)+c8)` → `cos(log(A+1))` ✓
- `A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`: set c4=0 → `A^c2*c3` with c2=2 → `-0.5475*A²` ✓
- `A*c0*exp(c1*t)` → `-0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t)` ✓
- **All three basis functions match!** **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 71: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1) + c9)`
- Has `cos(log(A+1))` ✓, `A*exp` ✓, but `exp(c3*t)` and `exp(c5*t)` are just time-dependent constants — no `A²`. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 81: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4)`
- `sin(A*c3+c4)` ≠ `cos(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]**
